<text>I absolutely love living here!  The staff is always so helpful, in anyway they can be.  From the office, Jordan, Eileen, and Hannah to the maintenance crew, of Brian, Richard, and Chris.  The residents are friendly.  The grounds are always kept clean, and well maintained.  The pool is beautiful, and I especially love, that it is salt water!

The apartments are new!  They are spacious, with high ceilings, and large windows.  They come with outlets, that allow for usb connection.  The kitchen has more than enough cupboard space, all within easy reach.   The bedrooms all have walk-in closets.  The bathrooms have double sinks.  The washer and dryer have their own hidden space.  The units come with heat and air-conditioning.  If you don't want to park in your garage, the parking area, is ample, and there is always a parking space available and close by, for you and your guests.  The area is quiet, and conveniently located, near 78.  Farmer's Market is every Saturday, and within walking distance.  Costco is just a little over a mile away, and the movie theaters are close by too.

If you have a dog, as I do, you don't have to run around looking for doggie bags.  The grounds, are overflowing with pet stations, for easy clean up.  We even have a self-service dog washing station :)

I am so glad I came to live here!

< text>
2020.09-20/SUN_1000; ALREADY a line for this place so you KNOW it's good! We ordered so much! Two mulitas - one made with birria and the other asada. Four queso tacos - two birria and two asada. Then four tacos Dorado - two birria and two asada.

I want to touch base on the smell of the delicious food from this place. It's entirely different. It's life your grandmother's house. Just the aroma alone from walking out of the room and back in, will make you speechless.

The mulitas MELTED IN MY MOUTH. I've had a lot of mulitas from other places and you know, they're okay but not like this! I ADORE their tortillas here. You can taste the homemade goodness coming from these tortillas. SO FREAKING GOOD. I can't even say enough about the quality and deliciousness of their food. It was so good that we inhaled all of our food! The tacos Dorado had the best light and crispy tortilla and it was stuffed! The queso tacos were the same! All of it! Just goodness in your mouth!

You definitely have to try them yourself! We arrived at 9:45 and got in line at 10 and there was already a line! One word for this place: fire. Enough said.</text>
